<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Football">Football</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Valencia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Football">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Valencia is also internationally famous for its football club, <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia CF</a>, one of the most successful clubs in Europe and La Liga, winning the <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">Spanish league</a> a total of six times including in 2002 and 2004 (the year it also won the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Cup</a>), and was a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> <a href="/wiki/Runner-up" title="Runner-up">runner-up</a> in 2000 and 2001. The club is currently owned by Peter Lim, a Singaporean businessman who bought the club in 2014. The team's stadium is the <a href="/wiki/Mestalla_Stadium" title="Mestalla Stadium">Mestalla</a>. The club's city rival, <a href="/wiki/Levante_UD" title="Levante UD">Levante UD</a>, also plays in La Liga and its stadium is <a href="/wiki/Estadi_Ciutat_de_Val%C3%A8ncia" title="Estadi Ciutat de Val√®ncia">Estadi Ciutat de Val√®ncia</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="American_Football">American Football</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Valencia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: American Football">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Valencia is the only city in Spain with two American football teams in <a href="/wiki/LNFA" class="mw-redirect" title="LNFA">LNFA Serie A</a>, the national first division: <a href="/wiki/Valencia_Firebats" title="Valencia Firebats">Valencia Firebats</a> and <a href="/wiki/Valencia_Giants" title="Valencia Giants">Valencia Giants</a>. The Firebats have been national champions four times and have represented Valencia and Spain in the European playoffs since 2005. Both teams share the Jard√≠n del Turia stadium.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Valencia_Street_Circuit_GT_Open.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/Valencia_Street_Circuit_GT_Open.jpg/220px-Valencia_Street_Circuit_GT_Open.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/Valencia_Street_Circuit_GT_Open.jpg/330px-Valencia_Street_Circuit_GT_Open.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/Valencia_Street_Circuit_GT_Open.jpg/440px-Valencia_Street_Circuit_GT_Open.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2942" data-file-height="1951" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Valencia_Street_Circuit_GT_Open.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Valencia_Street_Circuit" title="Valencia Street Circuit">Valencia Street Circuit</a></div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Motor_sports">Motor sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Valencia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Motor sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Once a year between 2008‚Äì2012 the European <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a> Grand Prix took place in the <a href="/wiki/Valencia_Street_Circuit" title="Valencia Street Circuit">Valencia Street Circuit</a>. Valencia is among (with <a href="/wiki/Barcelona" title="Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, <a href="/wiki/Porto" title="Porto">Porto</a> and <a href="/wiki/Monte_Carlo" title="Monte Carlo">Monte Carlo</a>) the only European cities ever to host Formula One World Championship Grands Prix on public roads in the middle of cities. The final race in <a href="/wiki/2012_European_Grand_Prix" title="2012 European Grand Prix">2012 European Grand Prix</a> saw home driver <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> win for <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a>, in spite of starting halfway down the field. The <a href="/wiki/Valencian_Community_motorcycle_Grand_Prix" title="Valencian Community motorcycle Grand Prix">Valencian Community motorcycle Grand Prix</a> <i>(Gran Premi de la Comunitat Valenciana de motociclisme)</i> is part of the Grand Prix motorcycle racing season at the Circuit Ricardo Tormo (also known as <i>Circuit de Valencia</i>) held in November. Periodically the Spanish round of the <a href="/wiki/Deutsche_Tourenwagen_Masters" title="Deutsche Tourenwagen Masters">Deutsche Tourenwagen Masters</a> touring car racing Championship (DTM) is held in Valencia.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rugby_League">Rugby League</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Valencia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Rugby League">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Valencia is also the home of the <a href="/wiki/Asociaci%C3%B3n_Espa%C3%B1ola_de_Rugby_League" class="mw-redirect" title="Asociaci√≥n Espa√±ola de Rugby League">Asociaci√≥n Espa√±ola de Rugby League</a>, who are the governing body for <a href="/wiki/Rugby_league" title="Rugby league">Rugby league</a> in Spain. The city plays host to a number of clubs playing the sport and to date has hosted all the country's home international matches.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> In 2015 Valencia hosted their first match in the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Rugby_league_European_Federation&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Rugby league European Federation (page does not exist)">Rugby league European Federation</a> C competition, which was a qualifier for the <a href="/wiki/2017_Rugby_League_World_Cup" title="2017 Rugby League World Cup">2017 Rugby League World Cup</a>. Spain won the fixture 40-30<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Districts">Districts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Valencia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Districts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Puente_del_Mar_-_Templetes_03.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Puente_del_Mar_-_Templetes_03.JPG/220px-Puente_del_Mar_-_Templetes_03.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Puente_del_Mar_-_Templetes_03.JPG/330px-Puente_del_Mar_-_Templetes_03.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Puente_del_Mar_-_Templetes_03.JPG/440px-Puente_del_Mar_-_Templetes_03.JPG 2x" data-file-width="4608" data-file-height="3072" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Puente_del_Mar_-_Templetes_03.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Pont de la Mar is one of the five existing medieval and early-modern bridges of the city</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Torres_quart.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Torres_quart.jpg/170px-Torres_quart.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="166" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Torres_quart.jpg/255px-Torres_quart.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Torres_quart.jpg/340px-Torres_quart.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2599" data-file-height="2533" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Torres_quart.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Towers of Quart, Christian city gate built between 1441 and 1460.</div></div></div>
